SELECT TOP(1) COALESCE(SUM([t].[TotalDebt]), 0.0) AS [TotalDebt], COUNT(*) AS [CustomerCount]
FROM (
    SELECT [c].[TotalDebt], 1 AS [Key]
    FROM [CUSTOMERS] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [c].[TotalDebt] > 0.0
) AS [t]
GROUP BY [t].[Key]
